# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Retry with Exponential Backoff Pattern Across Go Repos

## Your Task

Find Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus that implement retry with exponential backoff: the wait.ExponentialBackoff usage in k8s, the retrier implementations in grafana, and the backoff logic in prometheus remote write.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

## Summary

I found **10 key files** implementing retry with exponential backoff logic:

### **Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)**
- **staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/wait/backoff.go**: Core ExponentialBackoff function, Backoff struct, NewExponentialBackoffManager, and delay algorithm
- **pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff/exponential_backoff.go**: ExponentialBackoff struct for goroutine operations

### **Grafana (grafana/grafana)**
- **apps/provisioning/pkg/repository/git/repository.go**: defaultGitRetrier() using retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier with 8 attempts, 100ms initial delay, 5s max
- **pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/retry.go**: exponentialBackoffRetryer wrapping cenkalti/backoff/v4
- **pkg/util/retryer/retryer.go**: Direct exponential backoff implementation with minDelay doubling to maxDelay
- **pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/resources/retry_client.go**: Kubernetes wait.Backoff wrapper with 100ms initial, 2.0x factor, 8 steps

### **Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)**
- **storage/remote/queue_manager.go**: sendWriteRequestWithBackoff() for remote write retry with config-driven min/max bounds
- **tsdb/db.go**: exponential() function doubling duration each call, bounded by min/max
- **storage/remote/client.go**: Backoff error handling with Retry-After support
- **config/config.go**: MinBackoff (30ms default) and MaxBackoff (5s default) configuration

The Step() method implements the exponential backoff calculation.\\n\\n4. **delay Function (line 98)**: Core algorithm that calculates the next delay interval. It multiplies duration by the factor, applies jitter, and enforces cap limits.\\n\\n5. **NewExponentialBackoffManager Function (line 370)**: Creates a BackoffManager for managing exponential backoff with automatic reset after a specified duration.\\n\\nAlternatively, Kubernetes also maintains a separate exponential backoff implementation in Queue Manager (storage/remote/queue_manager.go, line 2022)**: The `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff()` function retries write requests with exponential backoff.
